#### Test TC015 Password storage security compliance
- **Test Code:** [TC015_Password_storage_security_compliance.py](./TC015_Password_storage_security_compliance.py)
- **Test Error:** The task to verify that user passwords are stored securely using bcrypt or Argon2 hashing algorithms is not fully completed. We created a test user with a known password and logged in successfully. However, the password is displayed in plain text ('1111111111') on the Employee List UI, which strongly suggests insecure storage or at least insecure display. Attempts to access backend or database to verify password hashing were unsuccessful due to lack of access or redirection to login. No evidence was found that passwords are stored securely using bcrypt or Argon2. Therefore, the task is incomplete and the system likely does not store passwords securely.
